</font><font color="#C0C0C0">Your aura of weapons rebounding disappears.
You play a wailing, discordant chord on Gorlityn the Tainted, directing the
 dissonant notes at</font><font color="#80FF80"> Leolamins.
</font><font color="#C0C0C0">The violent music rips</font><font color="#80FF80"> Leolamins </font><font color="#C0C0C0">asunder, whose lifeless corpse crumples to the
 ground.
